<exprlist>
  <COMMENT line1="1" col1="1" line2="1" col2="67" start="122" end="188"># Unexported, low-level function for fitting negative binomial GLMs</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="2" col1="1" line2="2" col2="1" start="243" end="243">#</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="3" col1="1" line2="3" col2="78" start="364" end="441"># Users typically call \code{\link{nbinomWaldTest}} or \code{\link{nbinomLRT}}</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="4" col1="1" line2="4" col2="71" start="485" end="555"># which calls this function to perform fitting.  These functions return</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="5" col1="1" line2="5" col2="66" start="606" end="671"># a \code{\link{DESeqDataSet}} object with the appropriate columns</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="6" col1="1" line2="6" col2="50" start="727" end="776"># added.  This function returns results as a list.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="7" col1="1" line2="7" col2="1" start="848" end="848">#</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="8" col1="1" line2="8" col2="23" start="969" end="991"># object a DESeqDataSet</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="9" col1="1" line2="9" col2="31" start="1090" end="1120"># modelMatrix the design matrix</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="10" col1="1" line2="10" col2="70" start="1211" end="1280"># modelFormula a formula specifying how to construct the design matrix</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="11" col1="1" line2="11" col2="46" start="1332" end="1377"># alpha_hat the dispersion parameter estimates</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="12" col1="1" line2="12" col2="71" start="1453" end="1523"># lambda the 'ridge' term added for the penalized GLM on the log2 scale</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="13" col1="1" line2="13" col2="64" start="1574" end="1637"># renameCols whether to give columns variable_B_vs_A style names</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="14" col1="1" line2="14" col2="66" start="1695" end="1760"># betaTol control parameter: stop when the following is satisfied:</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="15" col1="1" line2="15" col2="49" start="1816" end="1864">#   abs(dev - dev_old)/(abs(dev) + 0.1) &lt; betaTol</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="16" col1="1" line2="16" col2="67" start="1937" end="2003"># maxit control parameter: maximum number of iteration to allow for</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="17" col1="1" line2="17" col2="15" start="2058" end="2072">#   convergence</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="18" col1="1" line2="18" col2="65" start="2179" end="2243"># useOptim whether to use optim on rows which have not converged:</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="19" col1="1" line2="19" col2="63" start="2300" end="2362">#   Fisher scoring is not ideal with multiple groups and sparse</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="20" col1="1" line2="20" col2="23" start="2421" end="2443">#   count distributions</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="21" col1="1" line2="21" col2="66" start="2542" end="2607"># useQR whether to use the QR decomposition on the design matrix X</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="22" col1="1" line2="22" col2="45" start="2663" end="2707"># forceOptim whether to use optim on all rows</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="23" col1="1" line2="23" col2="61" start="2784" end="2844"># warnNonposVar whether to warn about non positive variances,</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="24" col1="1" line2="24" col2="59" start="2905" end="2963">#   for advanced users only running LRT without beta prior,</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="25" col1="1" line2="25" col2="42" start="3026" end="3067">#   this might be desirable to be ignored.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="26" col1="1" line2="26" col2="1" start="3147" end="3147">#</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="27" col1="1" line2="27" col2="58" start="3268" end="3325"># return a list of results, with coefficients and standard</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="28" col1="1" line2="28" col2="26" start="3389" end="3414"># errors on the log2 scale</COMMENT>
